#[acmd::acmd_func(
battle_object_category = BATTLE_OBJECT_CATEGORY_FIGHTER,
battle_object_kind = FIGHTER_KIND_CLOUD,
animation = "catch",
animcmd = "game_catch"
)]
fn cloud_catch_game(fighter: &mut L2CFighterCommon) {
acmd!({
    if (is_execute) {
        MotionModule::set_rate( 1.286);
    }
    frame(8)
    if (is_execute) {
        GrabModule::set_rebound( /*CanCatchRebound*/ true);
    }
    frame(9)
    if (is_execute) {
        MotionModule::set_rate( 1.0);
        CATCH(0, hash40("top"), 4.3, 0.0, 7.1, 0.0, 0.0, 7.1, 9.2, FIGHTER_STATUS_KIND_CAPTURE_PULLED, COLLISION_SITUATION_MASK_GA)
    }
    game_CaptureCutCommon();
    wait(2);
    if (is_execute) {
        grab(MA_MSC_CMD_GRAB_CLEAR_ALL)
        WorkModule::on_flag( /*Flag*/ FIGHTER_STATUS_CATCH_FLAG_CATCH_WAIT);
        GrabModule::set_rebound( /*CanCatchRebound*/ false);
    }
});
}

    frame(6)
    if (is_execute) {
        GrabModule::set_rebound( /*CanCatchRebound*/ true);
    }
    frame(7)
    if (is_execute) {
        CATCH(0, hash40("top"), 4.1, 0.0, 7.5, 0.0, 0.0, 7.5, 9.2, FIGHTER_STATUS_KIND_CAPTURE_PULLED, COLLISION_SITUATION_MASK_GA)
    }
    game_CaptureCutCommon();
    wait(2);
    if (is_execute) {
        grab(MA_MSC_CMD_GRAB_CLEAR_ALL)
        WorkModule::on_flag( /*Flag*/ FIGHTER_STATUS_CATCH_FLAG_CATCH_WAIT);
        GrabModule::set_rebound( /*CanCatchRebound*/ false);
    }
});
}

        WorkModule::on_flag( /*Flag*/ FIGHTER_BAYONETTA_STATUS_ATTACK_AIR_FLAG_CHECK_HOLD);
    }
    frame(41)
    if (is_execute) {
        sv_battle_object::notify_event_msc_cmd(0x2bfb02b69a as u64, false)
        AttackModule::clear_all();
    }
    frame(48)
    if (is_execute) {
        WorkModule::off_flag( /*Flag*/ FIGHTER_STATUS_ATTACK_AIR_FLAG_ENABLE_LANDING);
    }
    frame(70)
    if (is_execute) {
        sv_battle_object::notify_event_msc_cmd(0x2127e37c07 as u64, GROUND_CLIFF_CHECK_KIND_ALWAYS_BOTH_SIDES)
    }
});
}

#[acmd::acmd_func(
battle_object_category = BATTLE_OBJECT_CATEGORY_FIGHTER,
battle_object_kind = FIGHTER_KIND_BAYONETTA,
animation = "catch",
animcmd = "game_catch"
)]
fn bayonetta_catch_game(fighter: &mut L2CFighterCommon) {
acmd!({
    frame(6)
    if (is_execute) {
        GrabModule::set_rebound( /*CanCatchRebound*/ true);
    }
    frame(7)
    if (is_execute) {
        CATCH(0, hash40("top"), 4.3, 0.0, 6.6, 0.0, 0.0, 6.6, 10.2, FIGHTER_STATUS_KIND_CAPTURE_PULLED, COLLISION_SITUATION_MASK_GA)
    }
    game_CaptureCutCommon();
    wait(2);
    if (is_execute) {
        grab(MA_MSC_CMD_GRAB_CLEAR_ALL)
        WorkModule::on_flag( /*Flag*/ FIGHTER_STATUS_CATCH_FLAG_CATCH_WAIT);
        GrabModule::set_rebound( /*CanCatchRebound*/ false);
    }
});
}

#[acmd::acmd_func(

)]
fn simon_catch_game(fighter: &mut L2CFighterCommon) {

    frame(1)
    if (is_execute) {
        MotionModule::set_rate( 1.429);
        FighterAreaModuleImpl::enable_fix_jostle_area( 4, 6);
    }
    frame(9)
    if (is_execute) {
        GrabModule::set_rebound( /*CanCatchRebound*/ true);
    }
    frame(10)
    if (is_execute) {
        MotionModule::set_rate( 1.0);
        CATCH(0, hash40("top"), 4.3, 0.0, 6.6, 0.0, 0.0, 6.6, 9.2, FIGHTER_STATUS_KIND_CAPTURE_PULLED, COLLISION_SITUATION_MASK_GA)
    }
    game_CaptureCutCommon();
    wait(2);
    if (is_execute) {
        grab(MA_MSC_CMD_GRAB_CLEAR_ALL)
        WorkModule::on_flag( /*Flag*/ FIGHTER_STATUS_CATCH_FLAG_CATCH_WAIT);
        GrabModule::set_rebound( /*CanCatchRebound*/ false);
    }
});
}

#[acmd::acmd_func(

)]
fn richter_catch_game(fighter: &mut L2CFighterCommon) {
acmd!({
    frame(1)
    if (is_execute) {
        MotionModule::set_rate( 1.429);
        FighterAreaModuleImpl::enable_fix_jostle_area( 4, 6);
    }
    frame(9)
    if (is_execute) {
        GrabModule::set_rebound( /*CanCatchRebound*/ true);
    }
    frame(10)
    if (is_execute) {
        MotionModule::set_rate( 1.0);
        CATCH(0, hash40("top"), 4.3, 0.0, 6.6, 0.0, 0.0, 6.6, 9.2, FIGHTER_STATUS_KIND_CAPTURE_PULLED, COLLISION_SITUATION_MASK_GA)
    }
    game_CaptureCutCommon();
    wait(2);
    if (is_execute) {
        grab(MA_MSC_CMD_GRAB_CLEAR_ALL)
        WorkModule::on_flag( /*Flag*/ FIGHTER_STATUS_CATCH_FLAG_CATCH_WAIT);
        GrabModule::set_rebound( /*CanCatchRebound*/ false);
    }
});
}

    }
});

        WorkModule::on_flag( /*Flag*/ FIGHTER_KROOL_STATUS_SPECIAL_N_FLAG_SHOOT_IRONBALL);

        WorkModule::on_flag( /*Flag*/ FIGHTER_KROOL_STATUS_SPECIAL_N_FLAG_SHOOT_CANCEL);
    }
    frame(70)

        WorkModule::off_flag( /*Flag*/ FIGHTER_KROOL_STATUS_SPECIAL_N_FLAG_SHOOT_CANCEL);
        WorkModule::off_flag( /*Flag*/ FIGHTER_KROOL_STATUS_SPECIAL_N_FLAG_NO_SHOOT_CANCEL);
    }

}

        ATTACK(/*ID*/ 1, /*Part*/ 0, /*Bone*/ hash40("arml"), /*Damage*/ 7.0, /*Angle*/ 75, /*KBG*/ 70, /*FKB*/ 0, /*BKB*/ 70, /*Size*/ 4.0, /*X*/ 8.0, /*Y*/ 0.0, /*Z*/ 0.0, /*X2*/ LUA_VOID, /*Y2*/ LUA_VOID, /*Z2*/ LUA_VOID, /*Hitlag*/ 1.0, /*SDI*/ 1.0, /*Clang/Rebound*/ ATTACK_SETOFF_KIND_ON, /*FacingRestrict*/ ATTACK_LR_CHECK_SPEED, /*SetWeight*/ false, /*ShieldDamage*/ 0, /*Trip*/ 0.0, /*Rehit*/ 0, /*Reflectable*/ false, /*Absorbable*/ false, /*Flinchless*/ false, /*DisableHitlag*/ false, /*Direct/Indirect*/ true, /*Ground/Air*/ COLLISION_SITUATION_MASK_GA, /*Hitbits*/ COLLISION_CATEGORY_MASK_ALL, /*CollisionPart*/ COLLISION_PART_MASK_ALL, /*FriendlyFire*/ false, /*Effect*/ hash40("collision_attr_cutup"), /*SFXLevel*/ ATTACK_SOUND_LEVEL_M, /*SFXType*/ COLLISION_SOUND_ATTR_CUTUP, /*Type*/ ATTACK_REGION_PUNCH);

        ATTACK(/*ID*/ 3, /*Part*/ 0, /*Bone*/ hash40("arml"), /*Damage*/ 7.0, /*Angle*/ 75, /*KBG*/ 70, /*FKB*/ 0, /*BKB*/ 70, /*Size*/ 5.0, /*X*/ 2.5, /*Y*/ 0.0, /*Z*/ 0.0, /*X2*/ LUA_VOID, /*Y2*/ LUA_VOID, /*Z2*/ LUA_VOID, /*Hitlag*/ 1.0, /*SDI*/ 1.0, /*Clang/Rebound*/ ATTACK_SETOFF_KIND_ON, /*FacingRestrict*/ ATTACK_LR_CHECK_SPEED, /*SetWeight*/ false, /*ShieldDamage*/ 0, /*Trip*/ 0.0, /*Rehit*/ 0, /*Reflectable*/ false, /*Absorbable*/ false, /*Flinchless*/ false, /*DisableHitlag*/ false, /*Direct/Indirect*/ true, /*Ground/Air*/ COLLISION_SITUATION_MASK_GA, /*Hitbits*/ COLLISION_CATEGORY_MASK_ALL, /*CollisionPart*/ COLLISION_PART_MASK_ALL, /*FriendlyFire*/ false, /*Effect*/ hash40("collision_attr_cutup"), /*SFXLevel*/ ATTACK_SOUND_LEVEL_M, /*SFXType*/ COLLISION_SOUND_ATTR_CUTUP, /*Type*/ ATTACK_REGION_PUNCH);

    }
    frame(70)
    if (is_execute) {
        AttackModule::clear_all();
        MotionModule::set_rate( 2.0);
    }
    frame(86)
    if (is_execute) {
        MotionModule::set_rate( 0.33);
    }
    frame(90)
    if (is_execute) {
        WorkModule::on_flag( /*Flag*/ FIGHTER_PACKUN_STATUS_SPECIAL_HI_DIVE);
    }
});
}

#[acmd::acmd_func(
battle_object_category = BATTLE_OBJECT_CATEGORY_FIGHTER,
battle_object_kind = FIGHTER_KIND_PACKUN,
animation = "catch",
animcmd = "game_catch"
)]
fn packun_catch_game(fighter: &mut L2CFighterCommon) {
acmd!({
    frame(1)
    if (is_execute) {
        MotionModule::set_rate( 0.8333);
    }
    frame(5)
    if (is_execute) {
        GrabModule::set_rebound( /*CanCatchRebound*/ true);
    }
    frame(6)
    if (is_execute) {
        MotionModule::set_rate( 1.0);
        CATCH(0, hash40("top"), 4.3, 0.0, 6.6, 0.0, 0.0, 6.6, 12.5, FIGHTER_STATUS_KIND_CAPTURE_PULLED, COLLISION_SITUATION_MASK_GA)
    }
    game_CaptureCutCommon();
    wait(2);
    if (is_execute) {
        grab(MA_MSC_CMD_GRAB_CLEAR_ALL)
        WorkModule::on_flag( /*Flag*/ FIGHTER_STATUS_CATCH_FLAG_CATCH_WAIT);
        GrabModule::set_rebound( /*CanCatchRebound*/ false);
    }
});
